 There are widespread misconceptions about the location of Hindi in India's linguistic landscape
 yah desh kii 22 adhishuchet bhashaaon main se ek he
 According to each census data, it is also the most spoken language in the country
 haalanki hakeekat yah bhi he ki yah bhartiya rajyon main se zyaadaatar kii swaabhaavik bhashaa nahin he, jaise ki dakshin main kerala, tamilnadu, andhra pradesh, telugana, karnataka va puducheri; pashchim main goa, maharashtra or gujarat; uttar-pashchim main punjab va jammu-kashmir; purv main odisha va pashchim bengal or purvottar main sikkim, arunachal pradesh, mizoram, tripura, nagaland, manipur, meghalaya va assam
 These together make up 21 of the 30 states of the country
 mana jaataa he ki hindi himachal pradesh, uttarakhand, rajasthan, bihar, jharkhand va chhattisgarh jaise rajyon kii akeli yaa pramukh bhashaa he lekin in rajyon kii bhashaayi sanrachana ko bhi dhyaan se dekha jaae to un sabaki bhi apni mul kshetreey bhashaa he or unamem hindi ek sajhi antar-raji bhashaa ke taur par kaam karti he
 Hindi is often used as the second language of dialogue for people living in or passing through these states, then it seems to get a strong sense that it is the primary language of these states
 lekin yah baat tathyaatmak rup se sahi nahin he
 After the independence of the country in 1947, the question of conceptualizing any one language as our 'national language' has been repeatedly raised
 rajnatik partiyaan to swaabhaavik taur par rajnatik phaayde ke liye ise uthaati rahi hai
 But if a logical framework for this status is compared to the claim of Hindi against other languages, then it does not completely qualify
 viraasat ke mulya ke lihaaj se dekha jaae to tamil, kannada, telegu, malayalam, marathi, gujarati, sindhi, kashmiri, odissa, bangla, nepali va asamiya kii viraasat hindi se kahin zyada lambii he
 And if seen in terms of rapid growth, then Bhojpuri and even the tribal language Bhili has overtaken Hindi
 bhashaa ke sawaal main ulajhane par saamne aane vaali jatiltaaon kaa zyada spasht najariya hamaare samvidhan nirmaataaon ke paas tha
 In his hypothesis, India was a multilingual country in every sense, not a monolithic nation
 yah tathy, ki samvidhan kii aathvin anusuchee main 14 bhashaaon ko shaamil karne kaa faisla kiya gaya tha, is baat kii ore ingit karata he ki bharat ko kisi ek bhashaa ke saath baandhne kii koi ichha nahin thi
 However, there is no need to use all these factors to underestimate the growing role of Hindi in our mixed national life
 is samay, badhate antar-raji pravaas ko ek prabhavi bhashaayi sampark kii jarurat he
 Hindi fulfills this need with great efficiency because the grammar features of Hindi leave a lot of flexibility in terms of configuration
 aisa is vajah se bhi he ki hindi or telegu va kannada jaisi baaki bhashaaon main shabd bhandar kaa kaaphi bada saajha strot he
 Then, in terms of other countries, Hindi is being seen as the main language of India
 iske alaava shahari kshetron ke samajashaastra main hindi kii kaamkaaji upyogita zyada hone lagi he
 Due to all these functional and structural features, one may be forced to propose Hindi as India's number one language, but it would be more practical to declare it as 'second national language', and there are many reasons
 takneekee taur par 'duusari bhashaa' vah hoti he jise koi shaks ghar par nahin balki bazaar main, kaamkaaj kii jagah par or mahanagareey saamaajik daayaron main istemaal karata he, lekin na to ghar par or na hi apane saanskrithik aadan-pradaan ke kareebi daayre main
 Currently, there are about 800 living languages and dialects in India
 vyavhaar main to nahin lekin saidhantik rup se 799 bhashaaon ke log hindi kaa istemaal alag-alag str kii kushalta ke saath karte hai
 In this way, Hindi is the primary language of those who consider it as their mother tongue and the second language of those who consider another language as their mother tongue
 aise main agar 800 main se 799 bhashaa samudaay hindi ko duusari bhashaa maanate hon to bhi zyada se zyada vah hamaari duusari rashtriya bhashaa ho sakati he, isse zyada kuch bhi nahin
 Trying to do anything beyond this will be fundamentally undemocratic and will harm India's deep multilingual past and present
